## Last-Resort-Exceptions

- **Rebuttal #1: "Delete helios-cli now."** Rebutted: helios-cli has active code history. We must verify parity or archive instead of deleting. The residual gap is managed by target absorption.
- **Rebuttal #2: "Archive-not-deletion is insufficient."** Rebutted: Archival is the preferred path to preserve history on the remote while disabling write access, complying with BOUNDARY_OWNERS.
- **Rebuttal #3: "helios-cli cannot absorb exception."** Rebutted: The target `KooshaPari/helios-cli` can absorb the exception because it is the canonical repository for this boundary domain role.

No exceptions to the ARCHIVED verdict are granted.

## Restore-Command

```bash
# Disaster-recovery posture:
git clone https://github.com/KooshaPari/helios-cli.git /tmp/helios-cli-restore
# Verify bundle sha-256 (re-clone path is clean)
```
